# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
get everything in terms of sin and cos first
(using cotx = cosx / sinx rather than cotx = 1/tanx)

Whenever you have algebraic fractions being added/subtracted, whether a/b + c/d or a/b + c, combine them into one (as we can typically then use sin^ x + cos^2 x = 1 ^BNzWpVsz

c) prove that  ^ETywdZAT

a) Simplify sinθcotθsecθ
 ^3dJBMmvP

b) sinθcosθ(secθ + cosecθ) ^5cg69H7I

Solve the following equations in the interval 0≤θ≤360:
a) secθ = -2.5
b) cot2θ = 0.6 ^3aQg9PO4

Solve cotθ = 0, in the interval 0 ≤ θ ≤ 2π ^IeCdwSgM

Rewrite as powers of secθ, cosecθ or cotθ ^XxtzPyWM
